superfaction_setup romans_senate

default_hostile slave
default_hostile gauls
default_hostile carthage
default_hostile macedon

;;julii first mission should be to capture Pisna (Vallis_Arni)
mission_queue romans_julii
{
	major_reward 10 Take_City Pisna
}
;;brutii first mission should be to capture Taras (Tarentum)
mission_queue romans_brutii
{
	major_reward 10 Take_City Taras
}
;;scipii first mission should be to capture Messana (Siculia)
mission_queue romans_scipii
{
	major_reward 10 Take_City Messana
}
